### Post by oldfred on 2015-11-25
You are showing a Maxwell nVidia card. 
Are you using nomodeset?

If only Ubuntu you may not get grub. Have you installed in UEFI or BIOS boot mode?
If BIOS hold shift key, if UEFI press Escape Key.
But you probably need the fast boot (different than Windows fast start up) off in UEFI or you will not have time to press any keys during UEFI/BIOS screen. On my Asus I turned off fast boot until completely configured and then set to 3 sec, so I have time to do something if quick.

       At grub menu you can use e for edit, scroll to linux line and replace quiet splash with nomodeset.
How to set NOMODESET and other kernel boot options in grub2 - both BIOS liveCD & grub first boot ( also UEFI with grub) 
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1613132](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=1613132)
Possible boot options suggested by ubfan1
[URL="http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2184839&p=12871710#post12871710"]http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2184839&p=12871710#post12871710
[/URL]
Asus z97-A with nVidia GTX 970 Ubuntu  15.04
[http://askubuntu.com/questions/615896/ubuntu-15-04-uefi-cannot-install-blank-screen-no-signal?noredirect=1#615896](http://askubuntu.com/questions/615896/ubuntu-15-04-uefi-cannot-install-blank-screen-no-signal?noredirect=1#615896)

[URL="http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2184839&p=12871710#post12871710"]
[/URL]

### Post by oldfred on 2016-01-26
What version of Ubuntu?
Have you changed the settings in UEFI to UEFI only boot.
Are all drives gpt partitioned?
Did you turn off fast boot in UEFI. On my Asus I turned it off totally while configuring system. Set fast boot off for hard reboot or full power off, and set warm boot or reboot to 3 second delay, just so I had a bit of time to get to UEFI or one time boot key.

If not installing to drive seen as sda, you must use Something Else.
       Asus Motherboard Change UEFI from Windows (secure boot only) to other OS
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2245911](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2245911)
Minor problems with using an ASUS Z97-A Motherboard
[http://askubuntu.com/questions/503168/minor-problems-with-using-an-asus-z97-a-motherboard](http://askubuntu.com/questions/503168/minor-problems-with-using-an-asus-z97-a-motherboard)
[http://askubuntu.com/questions/554735/good-z97-motherboard-for-ubuntu](http://askubuntu.com/questions/554735/good-z97-motherboard-for-ubuntu)
BIOS only install Asus Z97-a

### Post by oldfred on 2016-01-26
Post this from terminal in live installer:

  sudo parted /dev/sda unit s print

One user posted UEFI screens.
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2245911&page=2&p=13136696#post13136696](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2245911&page=2&p=13136696#post13136696)

I also have screenshots of my Asus Z97-AR. While not same model of Asus, UEFI screens should be similar.

 Asus Motherboard Change UEFI from Windows (secure boot only) to other OS
[http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2298896](http://ubuntuforums.org/showthread.php?t=2298896)

### Post by oldfred on 2016-05-01
When it is working what does this show?
sudo lshw -C Disk -short

Sounds like one device has issues and prevents system from seeing all of them.
Or perhaps some setting in UEFI on device. Are drives set to AHCI?

### Post by stealthbyroot on 2016-05-02
Hi oldfred,

Looks like everything is working now.......Problem was.....
This MBO has two main SATA controllers: Intel and ASMedia. If I connect any device to ASMedia SATA controller everything is frozen. With Intel SATA controller all devices are running fine.So now all mine HD's and my DVD-ROM are running without any problem.
Technicality from the beginning ASMedia SATA controller was a problem.
Your help and effort is highly appreciated. Cheers.
